/// Logic
class Main
{
minPlayer = 2;
Seeker = 2;
Description = "players are divided into two teams: Hiders and Seekers. The objective for the Hiders is to stay hidden and survive within the games environment until the timer runs out. The Seekers must track down and capture all the Hiders before time expires";
_GameStart = false;
_GameStarted = false;
TimeLimit = 1600;
StartTimer = 20.0;
_CurrentTimer = 0.0;
_reset = false;
#SomeTests
_seekerID = 99999;
_seekerPlayer = null;
_startBarriers = null;
hidingTime = 60.0;
_HidingTimeStart = false;
_seekerTimer = null;
FPV = false;
_hasTimerStarted = false;
_lastTimer = self.TimeLimit;
_moving = false;
_stopallUI = false;
_HumanityWin = "";
_SeekerWin = "";

function StartGame()
{
#ResetUI
UI.SetLabelAll("MiddleCenter", "");

Game.Print("Game Started");
#Pick a random player and announce it to the other players
for (i in Range(0, self.Seeker, 1))
{
if (Network.IsMasterClient)
{
self._seekerID = 0;
self._seekerPlayer = null;
self._seekerID = Random.RandomInt(min: 0, max:Game.Humans.Count);
self._seekerPlayer = Network.Players.Get(Index: self._seekerID);
Network.SendMessageAll("The seeker is " + "<color=red> <b>" +  self._seekerPlayer.Name + "</b></color>");
Network.SendMessage(self._seekerPlayer, "setSeeker");
}
}

}


function OnCharacterSpawn(character)
{
if (character.IsMine && character.Type == "Human")
{
character.Team = "Blue";
character.SetSpecial("SmokeBomb");
character.SetWeapon("Blades");
character.CustomDamageEnabled = true;
character.CustomDamage = 0;
character.MaxGas = 999999;
character.CurrentGas = 999999;
character.MaxBlade = 0;
character.CurrentBlade = 0;
character.CurrentBladeDurability = 0;


}
}


function OnNetworkMessage(sender, message)
{
if (message != "setSeeker" && message != "EventA")
{
#ChatInteractions.Clear();
Game.Print("<color=orange>[Server] </color>" + "<color=white>" + message + "</color>");
}
if (message == "EventA")
{
self._seekerTimer = self.hidingTime + Time.GameTime;
self._HidingTimeStart = true;
}

if(message == "setSeeker")
{
_Character = Network.MyPlayer.Character;
Network.MyPlayer.Character.Position = new Vector3(-200.2029,79.45827,291.8377);
_Character.SetWeapon("AHSS");
_Character.Team = "Red";
_Character.MaxHealth = 9999999;
_Character.Health = 9999999;
_Character.MaxAmmoTotal = 999;
_Character.CustomDamage = 999;
_Character.MaxAmmoRound = 999;
_Character.CurrentAmmoLeft = 999;
_Character.CurrentAmmoRound = 999;
_Character.MaxGas = 999999;
_Character.CurrentGas = 999999;
Network.SendMessageAll("EventA");
}
}

function RestartGame()
{
Game.Print("Restarted game");
self._GameStart = false;
self._GameStarted = false;
}
function OnTick()
{
if (Game.GetMiscSetting("GlobalMinimapDisable") == true)
{
if (self.FPV)
{
Camera.FollowDistance = 0.0;
}
if (self._HidingTimeStart == true)
{
UI.SetLabelAll("MiddleCenter", "Hiding time : " + String.FormatFloat(self._seekerTimer - Time.GameTime, 2));
if (self._seekerTimer - Time.GameTime <= 0)
{
self._startBarriers = Map.FindMapObjectsByName("seekerBlock");
for (barrier in self._startBarriers)
{
barrier.Active = false;
}
self._HidingTimeStart = false;
self._hasTimerStarted = true;
}
}
else
{
UI.SetLabelAll("MiddleCenter", "");
}

numPlayers = Network.Players.Count;
if (!self._GameStart)
{
if (numPlayers >= self.minPlayer)
{
self._CurrentTimer = self.StartTimer + Time.GameTime;
self._GameStart = true;
}
else
{
_CurrentTimer = 99999;
UI.SetLabelAll("MiddleCenter", "Waiting for players...");
}
}

if (self._GameStart && numPlayers < self.minPlayer)
{
self._GameStart = false;
self.RestartGame();
}
if (self._GameStart && !self._GameStarted)
{
UI.SetLabelAll("MiddleCenter", "Match starting in : " + String.FormatFloat(self._CurrentTimer - Time.GameTime, 2));
}
if (self._CurrentTimer - Time.GameTime <= 0.0 && !self._GameStarted && self._GameStart)
{
self._GameStarted = true;
self.StartGame();
}
if (self._GameStarted)
{
if (self._hasTimerStarted)
{
self._lastTimer = self.TimeLimit + Time.GameTime;w
self._moving = true;
self._hasTimerStarted = false;
}
HumansAlive = Game.Humans.Count - self.Seeker;
if (self._moving && !self._stopallUI)
{
UI.SetLabelAll("TopCenter", "<color=light_green>Humans alive: </color>" + HumansAlive + "                  " + String.FormatFloat(self._lastTimer - Time.GameTime, 2) + "                  " + "<color=red>Seeker Alive: " + "</color>"  + self.Seeker);
}
elif (!self._moving && !self._stopallUI)
{
self._lastTimer = self.TimeLimit;
UI.SetLabelAll("TopCenter", "<color=light_green>Humans alive: </color>" + HumansAlive + "                  " + self._lastTimer + "                  " + "<color=red>Seeker Alive: " + "</color>"  + self.Seeker);
}
if (HumansAlive == 0 && self._HumanityWin != "X")
{
UI.SetLabelAll("TopCenter", "<color=light_green>Humans alive: </color>" + HumansAlive + "                  " + "FINISH" + "                  " + "<color=red>Seeker Alive: " + "</color>"  + self.Seeker);
self.ResetGame(2);
}

if (self._lastTimer - Time.GameTime  <= 0 && self._moving && self._SeekerWin != "X")
{
self.ResetGame(1);
UI.SetLabelAll("TopCenter", "<color=light_green>Humans alive: </color>" + HumansAlive + "                  " + "FINISH" + "                  " + "<color=red>Seeker Alive: " + "</color>"  + self.Seeker);
}
}
}
else
{
UI.SetLabelAll("MiddleCenter", "<color=red>Disable the minimap to play this gamemode</color>");
}
}

function ResetGame(value)
{
if (self._reset == false)
{
self._CurrentTimer = self.StartTimer + Time.GameTime;
self._reset = true;
Game.End(20);
}
_stopallUI = true;
if (value == 2)
{
UI.SetLabelAll("MiddleCenter", "Seeker won");
self._SeekerWin = "X";
}
else
{
UI.SetLabelAll("MiddleCenter", "Humans won");
self._HumanityWin = "X";
}
#self.RestartGame();
}
}










extension ChatInteractions
{
function Clear()
{
for (i in Range(0, 15, 1))
{
Game.Print("");
}
}
}
